          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<div role="heading" class="comment-header" aria-level="2">
        <div>
          <a class="comment-link" href="?id=1410191#c5">Comment 5<!----></a>

          
        by

It seems that the crash occurs because the size of the buffer "d" is smaller than the last parameter of sw::clear.



<span class="line"><!---->It seems that the crash occurs because the size of the buffer "d" is smaller than the last parameter of sw::clear.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The area.extent.width is controllable, it is the width size of the canvas.



<span class="line"><!---->The area.extent.width is controllable, it is the width size of the canvas.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





bool Blitter::fastClear(const void *clearValue, vk::Format clearFormat, vk::Image *dest, const vk::Format &viewFormat, const VkImageSubresourceRange &subresourceRange, const VkRect2D *renderArea)



<span class="line"><!---->bool Blitter::fastClear(const void *clearValue, vk::Format clearFormat, vk::Image *dest, const vk::Format &amp;viewFormat, const VkImageSubresourceRange &amp;subresourceRange, const VkRect2D *renderArea)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





...



<span class="line"><!---->...<!----></span>



<br>





			uint8_t *d = slice;



<span class="line"><!---->			uint8_t *d = slice;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





			switch(viewFormat.bytes())



<span class="line"><!---->			switch(viewFormat.bytes())<!----></span>



<br>





			{



<span class="line"><!---->			{<!----></span>



<br>





			case 4:



<span class="line"><!---->			case 4:<!----></span>



<br>





				for(uint32_t i = 0; i < area.extent.height; i++)



<span class="line"><!---->				for(uint32_t i = 0; i &lt; area.extent.height; i++)<!----></span>



<br>





				{



<span class="line"><!---->				{<!----></span>



<br>





					ASSERT(d < dest->end());



<span class="line"><!---->					ASSERT(d &lt; dest-&gt;end());<!----></span>



<br>





					sw::clear((uint32_t *)d, packed, area.extent.width);  // [1]



<span class="line"><!---->					sw::clear((uint32_t *)d, packed, area.extent.width);  // [1]<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





sw::clear works like memset, possible heap overflow (or oob write) caused by count exceeding buffer size.



<span class="line"><!---->sw::clear works like memset, possible heap overflow (or oob write) caused by count exceeding buffer size.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void clear(uint32_t *memory, uint32_t element, size_t count)



<span class="line"><!---->void clear(uint32_t *memory, uint32_t element, size_t count)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





#if defined(_MSC_VER) && defined(__x86__) && !defined(MEMORY_SANITIZER)



<span class="line"><!---->#if defined(_MSC_VER) &amp;&amp; defined(__x86__) &amp;&amp; !defined(MEMORY_SANITIZER)<!----></span>



<br>





	__stosd((unsigned long *)memory, element, count);					  // [2]



<span class="line"><!---->	__stosd((unsigned long *)memory, element, count);					  // [2]<!----></span>



<br>





#elif defined(__GNUC__) && defined(__x86__) && !defined(MEMORY_SANITIZER)



<span class="line"><!---->#elif defined(__GNUC__) &amp;&amp; defined(__x86__) &amp;&amp; !defined(MEMORY_SANITIZER)<!----></span>



<br>





	__asm__ __volatile__("rep stosl"



<span class="line"><!---->	__asm__ __volatile__("rep stosl"<!----></span>



<br>





	                     : "+D"(memory), "+c"(count)



<span class="line"><!---->	                     : "+D"(memory), "+c"(count)<!----></span>



<br>





	                     : "a"(element)



<span class="line"><!---->	                     : "a"(element)<!----></span>



<br>





	                     : "memory");



<span class="line"><!---->	                     : "memory");<!----></span>



<br>





#else



<span class="line"><!---->#else<!----></span>



<br>





	for(size_t i = 0; i < count; i++)



<span class="line"><!---->	for(size_t i = 0; i &lt; count; i++)<!----></span>



<br>





	{



<span class="line"><!---->	{<!----></span>



<br>





		memory[i] = element;



<span class="line"><!---->		memory[i] = element;<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>





#endif



<span class="line"><!---->#endif<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>

```c++

The reason the buffer bounds overflow is because of the area.extent.height of the for loop. [1]



<span class="line"><!---->The reason the buffer bounds overflow is because of the area.extent.height of the for loop. [1]<!----></span>

```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





gl.renderbufferStorage(gl.RENDERBUFFER, gl.RG8UI, 1304, 2041);

<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

This value comes from the last parameter of the gl.renderbufferStorage in poc.



<span class="line"><!---->This value comes from the last parameter of the gl.renderbufferStorage in poc.<!----></span>

The rowPitchBytes is calculated through the Image::rowPitchBytes method, and this value was 0x4b0 when debugging. [2]



<span class="line"><!---->The rowPitchBytes is calculated through the Image::rowPitchBytes method, and this value was 0x4b0 when debugging. [2]<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Fix clearing of extended dirty bits in draw calls



<span class="line"><!---->Fix clearing of extended dirty bits in draw calls<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When syncing all dirty bits (i.e. in draw calls), the extended dirty



<span class="line"><!---->When syncing all dirty bits (i.e. in draw calls), the extended dirty<!----></span>



<br>





bits were not cleared.  This caused the extended dirty bits to be



<span class="line"><!---->bits were not cleared.  This caused the extended dirty bits to be<!----></span>



<br>





resynced every time.



<span class="line"><!---->resynced every time.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
